 
Ngimfunge EseNgoleleni! 
p.B. Maphumulo 
 
 
     


 
Amazwi Okubonga 
Ngizothatha leIi thuba ngibonge kuMveIinqangi uMninimandla onke ongigcinile kwaze kwafika lolu suku lokufezeka kwesifiso sozalo esimaqondana nokubhalwa kwale ncwadi equkethe umlando walo. Ngizizwa nginethemba eligijima phakathi emizweni nasemithanjeni yami lokuthi luzoyemukela ngesasasa ngeso lokuyithokozela kwazise phela ukuthi isifiso esinjengaleso sasizwakala siyiphupho nemfeketho nje eminyakeni ephambili ungakaqalwa nokuqoqwa nje 10 mlando. 





Mangiqale ngokuthi sekuqala ukuba wukhondolo oluyinjwayezi ukuzwa ukuthi abantu besibongo simbe bazohlangana ndawana thizeni, ngalusuku I\lmbe nangesikhathi leso esimisiwe. Kafushane nje inhloso yalokho kusuke kungukukhuthaza ukwazana kozalo 1010 kanye nokuqhwanda ulwazi olumaqondana narnasiko, usikompiIo, imikhuba kanye nezinkolelo zabantu baleso sibongo olusuke seluthanda ukushabalala. Kodwa okukhulu kunakho konke kusuke kuwukutatulula umlando waso ophathelene nemvelaphi yaso ngokoIibo lwaso kusukela kokhulukhulwana, okhokho, omkhulu nogogo lixhumeke njalo ike tango lokuzalana nokwelamana kuze kufike esizukulwaneni leso esikhona. Lolu khondolo luhle kakhulu. Ludinga ukukhuthazwa bese kuthi labo bantu abazihluphile badela yonke imisebenzi yabo namagugu abo ngenhloso yokuzokwethamela lesi sithangami sokushiyelana ulwazi nokuncelisana umbele ogwanse ngalolu hlobo, bona-ke bazishayele eIikhulu ihlombe leli kuze kwemukelane imimmemo ezihosheni. Ingani phela ekuhlanganeni bedingida ngezomlando wesibongo. sabo basuke befakazela Iesi sisho esithi, "isizwe esingenawo amasiko sifana nomuthi ongenazimpande." Siphinde siqhubeke futhi lesi sisho urna sekuthiwa, "isizwe esingena- 
. mlando sifana nomuthi ongenawo amaqabunga." 
Enye inhlosongqangi yokukhuthaza inhlanganQ nobunye bozalo obunjengalobu, wukuqondisisa kabanzi izithakazelo ezib"a nokuhlangana ezibongweni ezingefani kanye nalezo enisuke nizitshela ukuthi kaninabudlelwano nazo. Isibonelo esihle salokhu ngakolwami uhlangothi yisibongo sakwaNkwanyana. Lesi sibongo kasiveIi oIibeni Iwesibongo sakwaMaphumulo, kodwa ngethuka isimanga ngelinye iIanga ngesikhathi ngeshela intokazi yalesi sibongo engu-Edmara ngenkathi ingitshela ukuthi 






11. 
ngingumfowabo ngakho-ke akukho ukuganana, ukuganiselana nokwakha ubuhlobo noma ngandlelani kulezi zibongo ngoba vele zihlobene. Ngathatha ngokuthi Ie ntokazi iyangichitha nje ngezindlela eziphansi kanti qha, iqinisile ngempela. lsisekelo saleli qiniso sengize 'ngisithole ngezaguga zaso lesi sibongo sakwaNkwanyana. Ngalesi sibonelo ngisagcizelela khona njalo ukubaluleka kokubamba imihlangano yozaIo ngoba kuvulana imiqondo. lngani phela elwazini olunjengalolo-ke usheshe azihlalukele obala umuntu ohlobene naye ukuze kugwemeke ingozi yokuganana nokuganiselana kwezihlobo obekubangelwa wukungabi nalwazi nosekungaze kukudonsele imikhokha emibi emathongeni kumbe emadlozini akini, ulaka lwabaphansi kanye nesigcwagcwa kumbe imishophi ethile. lngani phela ngesikhathi senisondelana ngokocansi nalowo enihlobene naye seningaze nizale izingane eziyizidalwa ngokukhubazeka ngokwengqondo noma ngokomzimba, uma zingabanga ngamahlongandlebe. 
Nathi-ke siwuzalo nabantu besibongo sakwaMaphumulo abathakazelwa kuthiwe Mgobode, Zulu, Zukuzela, Zikode, Cwalide, Masiyane, Lubheleni, Dubandlela, Mashimane, njlI. Sabona kungumqondo owephusile nonobuhlakani ukwakha umfelandawonye wokuvuselela umlando wesibongo sakithi kanye nokuzihlupha ngokucobelelana ngamasiko, usikompiIo, imikhuba kanye nezinkolelo zakithi. Yingakho-ke nje kusukela onyakeni ka-1987 saqala ukuharnba imihlangano, nezingqungquthela zokuqoqa imali yokwakhiwa kwetshe lesikhumbuzo sikaMashimane nokushiyelana ulwazi olunzulu olumaqondana nakho konke okungamagugu esizwe sakoMashimane njengokuzalana kwethu. 
Ngenxa yesasasa nenkuthalo yozalo ngale mibuthano, sigcine sesiphembe amaziko ahlukene sagcoba nezinsika zawo ezindaweni eziningi kuleli lengabadi. Phakathi kwawo ngibala elikhulu kunawo wonke leli laseNgoleleni nokuyilona okuqanjwe ngalo isihloko sale ncwadi njengoba sithi, "Ngimfunge eseNgoleleni!" Amanye esingawabala kule ngosi yileli laseMdumezulu (eMbumbulu), elakubaPhehli (eManzimtoti), elaseFolweni, elaseziChwayini (eNsuze), elaseNtshiwe nakwaGeqindlebe . (eBhamshela), elasoVanzini (kwaMaphumulo), elaseNgudwini (ngaseMarideni). lsihlava sozalo esangena kusemnandi kusenjalo senza kwabalukhuni satshe ukuqhubeka nokuphemba amanye amaziko njengoba amabombo ethu ayesazolibhekisa eSamungu, eMngwenya kanye nakuleli 
ii 

laseMamba (ngaseNtumeni) nokuyilapho wonke urn lando wesibongo sakithi uqala khona Ngingelilibale futhi neziko laseMaqongqo (ngaseMgungundlovu) lapho kunesizwe sakwaMaphumulo esingangenzaIa yotshani. Kukhona namanye futhi amaziko arnancane ebesike siwahambele okungaphela iphepha uma ngingathi ngizama ukuwabala, kodwa ngaphezu kwalokho akumele ngilishiye ngaphandle leli laseHammersdale. Kuwo wonke la maziko besifike siphathwe ngezandla ezifudumele nezigcwele uthando okungangoba nemicimbi yethu beyiqhubeka ngobunono bekati kuwona. 
Nokho kumele ngikubalule futhi ukuthi kuzo zonke izikhathi ezimnandi zemikhosi yozaIo, bekuye kube neziwombe ezinzima ezazibanga ukuphazamiseka Phakathi kokunye ngizobala isiwombe somhlangano owawukubaPhehli ngo-1990 lapho isimo nomoya wezepolitiki owawuvunguza ngale minyaka waludunga lolu bumbano walwehlukanisa phakathi. Lapha ngibhekise kubantu abake bahlasela ngebhaxa lokuthi bebecabanga ukuthi wumhlangano wenhlangano yimbe yezombusazwe lena. 
Kwasibeka inkarnbabeyibuza futhi ukukhothama kwenkosi uMhlabunzima Joseph Maphumulo ngoba kwaphazamisa izinWelo eziningi esingabala phakathi kwazo leyo yokwakha idlinza lenkosi uMashimane uMashimane kaDubandlela libe sesimeni setshe lesikhumbuzo okwakuyokuthi kulo kugujwe imikhosi yozaIo yaminyaka yonke njengoba kwenziwa emikhosini yeSiIo samabandla esesakhothama uShaka kaSenzangakhona ngenyanga kaMandulo kwaDukuza Lokhu sasiyokwenza ngakho ngoba siqhakambisa uMashimane ngoba nguyena kuphela emakhosini ozalo owaba negalelo ngokumisa ubukhosi besizwe sakwaMaphumulo ngesikhathi izinto zishisisa okweseko eziko. Nokho kuyangithokozisa ukubona ukuthi lusekhona uthando kwabaningi okungathi ngokunikezelana lwedlulele nakulabo abangakayiboni Ie ndlela ehanjwayo, kuholele ekutheni iphupho labaningi ngetshe lesikhumbuzo Iigcine selibe yiqiniso. Mangiphinde ngisho ukuthi isiWava esibangelwa ukungaziboni izinto ngaso Iinye siwuzalo yisona esigcine sidale ukuphazamiseka kwentuthuko" nenqubekelaphambili okungabe sesiyizuzile saze saba ngabanqobi lesi sizwe sakoMashimane. Ababaningi nokho ababhebhezeli bale nto kanye noNgoma-uyayona, yidlanzana nje labantu abazibona bengconywana bona ngesingabo kodwa thina esikwaziyo ukuzibona izinto esibabona bengabalulekile njengoba bona bezitshela kurnbe becabanga 
iii 




Ukubonga kwami kuwya enkosini u-Amos Khenqe yakhona impela eNgoleleni ekhothame ngonyaka ka-1999 emva kokugula isikhathi eside. Mangisho nje ngithi Ie nkosi ngazana nayo ngomhiaka 6 kuNcwaba ngo1989 emhlanganweni owabe usesikoleni eMthombeni lapho eyaze yakhipha isiklabhu sayo esingangentondolo ithi ihlabisa abozalo IwakwaMaphumulo olwaluqhamuka eShowe, okwakungumnewethu uHolg-divine uSinakanaka, uPhefeni Goodluck kanye nami Patrick oBhekizenw zikaMnyamasitezi. 

Udlame lwezepolitiki lwaphinde lwasigqema udume lwengozi engeqiwa ntwala ngokusephuca umnewethu uMqolo uWalter ngoNhlangulana ka-1998 nokunguyena owabe eyinsika yeziko laseMdumezulu. Phakathi kwamaqhawe esizigqaja ngawo siyisizwe sakwaMaphumulo ngingabala ubaba uMbokode uJacob okunguyena owabe eyinsika yeziko elikubaPhehli njengoba wabe evame ukubizela imihlangano yozalo ehholo eliseBhekulwandle eManzimtoti. Okubuhlungu nokudabukisayo wukuthi nayo Ie nsizwa endala yasishiya emhlabeni onyakeni ka-2000 yathathwa wukugula okwakuye kuyihlasele izikhawu kubuye kuyidedele. Angiwukhohlwa neze umhlangano wokuvala unyaka owaba ngundabuzekwayo eyabe lwubizele kulo leli ziko wathatha izinsuku ezintathu kusukeia ngomhlaka 19 kuze kube ngumhlaka 21 kUZibandlela ka-1997. Nawe futhi sithi uphumule ngokuthula Mashimane omkhulu ngokuba imisebenzi yakho iyokulandela. 

Omunye ukhukhulelangoqo womhlangano owaba sematheni kwaba yilowo owabe useziChwayini ngomhlaka-12 kuMfumfu ka-1997. Kulo mhlangano isizwe sakwaMaphumulo sasiwukhumbintethe sembethe amaqele wena owabona inkasa yezinkumbi nxashane zivunywe wuhlaza. Phakathi kwezinye izilomo esingeke sazilibala ezibe negalelo kule mihlangano yozalo, singabala umfowethu ongasekho owedlule nodlame lwamatekisi ngo-1999, uBongani uBoy owabe evame ukubizela umhlangano wozalo ezikweni lamaZikode elaliseHammersdale. 

MaZukuzela amahle, seniyongixolela kakhulu uma kuyangoba kukhona abanye enibaziyo ukuthi sebashona ababamba eIikhulu iqhaza leIi' entuthukweni yozalo IwakwaMaphumulo kodwa engingasakwazanga ukufinyelela ekubaluleni amagama abo. Kodwa noma kunjalo muzi

kulapho ebengibuye ngitomule kumbe ngitatulule khona ulwazi olunzuIu Iwemilando emidala ezifana nalena kaMagema Fuze ebizwa ngokuthi yi "The Black People and Ht7zence They Came", ehunyushelwe nasolimini lwesiZulu yaziwa ngesihloko esithi, "Abantu AbaMnyama Lapho Bavela Ngakhona". Ezinye izincwadi ezibe nom lando omuhle kaMashimane yile miqingo ka-A. T. Bryant i "Olden Times in Zululand and Natal" " nalena ethi "11ze Zulu People." Olunye ulwazi ngaleli qhawe ngiluvumbulule kwiHistorical Museum eseMgungundlovu engezansana kancane kweMarket square. Izincwadi ezibe wusizo lapha yilezi, ekaGrant "izibongo of the Zulu Chiefs (Vo1.3 no 3), ekaHolden "Past and future of the Kaffir Races", ekaLeslie, "Among the Zulus and amaThonga", ekaMason "Life with the Zulus of Natal", ekaMcKenzie "Mission life among the Zulu Kaffirs, ekaSamuelson L.H. "Zululand, its Traditions, Legends and Customs.' EkaSamuelson, R.C. "Long, Long Ago", ekaShooter "The Kaffirs of Natal". Kukuyo futhi Ie Historical Museum lapho ngahlangabezana nezibongo zikaMashimane, sengibala. konk~ nebinza lomlando osesiqeshini samakhosi ayishumi nantathu ngaphansl kwesihloko esithi, "The Origin and the Rise of the Maphumulo Clan under Chief Mashimane Son of Dubandlela up until His First clash with ChiefMakhutha Son of Makhanya on the South Coastal Region of Natal, " njengokulandiswa nguSiwehle Maphumulo emkhosini wokukhunjulwa kwamaqhawe avelele kwelengabadi owabe ukwaDukuza ngonyaka ka1928. Phakathi kwazo uze wangeboleka nencwadi eyaziwa ngokuthi "Uphoko" eyabhalwa nguDokotela Reggie Sipho Khumalo ongumsakazi wodumo lwezinhlelo zezolimo, ~asiko nemilando yakwazulu oKhozini FM. viii 


ohlelweni lwangoNtulikazi ka- 1984 olwalwaziwa ngokuthi "Sidla Ngoludala" olwalushayelwa nguMsakazi osewathatha umhlalaphansi uThokozani Ernest Mandlenkosi Nene (uGxabalembadada). Lolu hlelo lwalunikezwe isihloko esithi, "lmvelaphi nokudabuka kwesibongo sakwaMaphumulo," kodwa egxile kakhulu ebuhlotsheni obukhona phakathi kukazulu noMaphumulo njengoba phela ezithakazelweni zakwaMaphumulo siqhamuka futhi isibongo sakwazulu. 
KunomkhuJu futhi obizwa ngokuthi nguSikhumbasengwe Maphumulo waseMsimbazi uma uqonde ngaseMfume. Ube negalelo elikhuJu nesineke esiyinqaba ukusilandisa ngaleli qhawe elinguMashimane kaDubandlela. 
NgingakaIubeki phansi usiba lwami mangibonge futhi ulwazi engilucoshe kubaba uThamsanqa E. SithoJe encwadini yakhe enesihJoko esithi "IzilhakazeJo nezibongo zakwazulu." Mangilimise ngesihloko elokuthi I~ ncwadi-ke yona inobuciko obehlukile nobedlulele bayo yodwa nje oIwazini olwejwayelekile Iwezibongo nezithakazelo uma sekuya ngakulo mkhakha obizwa ngokuthi yizithopho. 
Ngokuqhubeka kwesasasa lOkwethanyelwa kwemihlangano yozalo, kuhambe kwahamba kwaze kwafika eqophelweni lokuba size sibe nongoti bozalo abangabathwebuli bezithombe zevideo. Kule Roll call kumbe Ie register engiyibizayo njengamanje akumele ngikushiye ngaphandJe nawe futhi Mashimane wasesiNqawunqawini. Ngisho wena Bongani Maphumulo wakwaSection C kuMhlanga Road kwaMashu. Lincomeka kakhulu iqhaza obulibambile kule mihlangano yozalo njengensizwa enekhono eliyisimangaliso kulo msebenzi. Sengathi ibhizinisi lakho i "BP Studio, Video & Photography' Iingakhula Iidlondlobale Iize Iificwe nayizizukulwane ngezizukulwane ezizayo. 
Ngisasho amazwi afanayo nakuwe futhi Phindela Maphumulo owaziwa ngelika "Kiss Mantombazane" kwezoMaskandl izinsizwa nezintokazi. Yaze yabuya emazweni impi yenkosi uShaka lapho yabe kade ihlasele khona Yabuya ihlomulile ngempela futhi ngoba yabuya nochithi-mafusini wemfuyo enonophele yodwa eyabe ivele yembethe imfunda yotshani obuluhlaza ewe kwesweleke amaqele namadlelo. Inkosi isithumele omunye wezinsila zayo ukuba iyobiza uDubandlela kanye nalesi sigejana sezinsizwa amatasatasa nazo. Nembala ume umsebenzi okwesikhashana sekuyiwa esithangamini sokuqulwa kwecala ngaphansi kwesihlahla somlahlankosi. ISAHlUKO 3 
Sibuye Ze Ngasitha 
Sesiside kakhulu manje isikhathi selokhu uDubandlela ehambile nethimba lelo ukuyolanda izinkomo zenkosi phesheya koThukela. Kufanele ngabe kudala ebuyile. ISilo sesize sathuma uZihlandlo ukuba ake ayomhlolela isimo atholisise kahle ukuthi uDubandlela lona ngabe usebanjwe yini. Nembala aphume uZihlandlo alandele umkhondo kaDubandlela kodwa afice itshe selome inhlama. 
     "Ngiyile Ngasitha lapho inkosi yami ibingithume khona. Ezibuhlungu nje ngezokuthi bengiphume inqina kamabuyaze ... " Akhulume kanjena uZihlandlo kube sengathi kuphithana ikhanda kuShaka. Ngokukhulu ukushesha usegqunqe wamnyama ebusweni okwezulu lizoduma. Amehlo abe bomvu alokoze inhlansi yomlilo. . 
     "Kahle ukungethusa wena Zihlandlo. Ake uchaze wenabe ngizwe kahle." Sekusho iLembe selinyukubele kakhulu kunakuqala lingasabhe- 
keki nasebusweni. 	. 
     "Imilobo yezinyawo ikhombisa ngokusobala ukuthi uDubandlela lona ufinyelele yena ezibukweni ebithena inkosi makayowela kulo, kodwa imilobo yezinyawo ezibuyayo ikubeka kucace ukuthi akazange nhlobo awele lapho, ukuze ashes he afinyelele phesheya koThukela." 
     "Pho-ke manje uphi? Ngabe uphume walibhekisaphi?" Kwakusabuza lona njalo iLembe limangele. Isifuba salo lesi sesigubhazela ngenxa yentukuthelo. 
     "Impela iyindida indaba kaDubandlela Zulu eliphezulu. Bheka ngoba ngiqhubekile-ke nami nohambo ngaze ngayofika lapho phesheya koThukela ebengicabanga ukuthi ngingase ngimelamele khona, kodwa lutho. Ngifice itshe selome inhlama, kwankomo lezo zingasafaniswa nangalukhalo." 
     "Hheyi madodal Yini lena angenza yona uDubandlela? Inkosi impela angithukuthele ngiyaqhuma. Inhliziyo yami kuthi ayiphume ngembobo yendle dadewethu kababa. Ngithi uzongifunda angiqonde uDubandlela, abakhwekazi bheka. Ngithi njengamanje futha uphondo Zihlandlo luhlabe umkhosi lubize isizwe sami ngokushesha enhla nasezansi kwelikaMthaniya." . Kwasho iLembe libhodla umlilo ngenxa yentukuthelo.

Kwabe alushilo uphondo Iwansondo. Lwalusho kuze kube sengathi lubhadla emathunjini inkosi impela. Ngokuphazima kweso abantu benkosi base benyamfuka nje koMkhulu wena owabona izimpethu zendlovu. 
Ngaleyana phesheya koThukela abalandeli bakaDubandlela bazibona sebesekhaya nje nakhu phela balifica liyikwampunzi idla emini. Nezizwana abazifice lapha sebevele bazigwinya bazifukamela zaba' ngaphansi kweso likaDubandlela. Izizwe ezase zibanjwe yizikhwepha zikaDubandlela ngale minyaka kwabe kungesaseMangangeni emaKhabeleni. Kusukela eMgungundlovana, eMsinga, eNtunjambili kwehle njalo kuze kuyofika ezansi neNonotL yizindawo ezase zikhonyelwa yinkunzi eyodwa lezo, uDubandlela. 
"Mazikode amahle, sesifike eKuphumuleni-ke uma ngabe sesilapha. 
Zizweni nisekhaya-ke bantu bami. Nehlukene noShaka. Ngeke aze anithole ngisho esethanda kangakanani. Imifula okumele ayiwele uma ngabe eza lapha inezingwenya kanti namahlanze okumele awadabule anezinyoka ezesabekayo. Nibonile nani ukuthi kube ngumqansa ongakanani ukufmyelela kwethu kuleli. Kuze kwadingeka ukuba sisebenzise amazibuko akude ebe ecashile njalo futhi." Sekusho uDubandlela.

Amakhosi amabili awabuselani. Ngokunjalo futhi izinkunzi ezimbili zingehlale sibayeni sinye.      "Mazikode amahle, ngihlezi phezu kodengezi luseziko njengoba nisazi-ke nani isimo. OkaSenzangakhona usengase angihlasele noma yinini kusukela manje. Ngibona sekuyiso-ke manje lesi isikhathi sokuba ngilifulathele leli ngiqhubeke nohambo." Sekusho uMashimane.

Sikhulule thina esesiyizaguga mzukulu sisale kulo leli." Kwaphawula urnxhiliba wesalukazi uNonsindolo esabe sithefuya futhi sinqimfoza senziwa yiphika.

Ozwa kuthi akasale, ukhululekile kulokho. Obona kufanele abambelele emchilweni wami futhi kusuka ngaphakathi kuye lokho, wamukelekile ngihamba nabahambayo mina."

Kuthe noma beyinohlonze kangako ingxoxo yokubonisana phakathi kukaNobanda noMashimane, kodwa wabuye wafikelwa ngomunye umcabango uMashimane wokuyishaya indiva imibono yomnewabo. Kunokuba abalekelane nenkosi uShaka, wabona kufanelekile ukuba asondelane naye kakhulu kunakuqala manje. Kungabe yini okwase kumbusa engqondweni nokwabe kumnika umdlandla ongaka? Akwaziwa, kodwa iqiniso lona liwvela khona maduze nje. Wafika seliqala ukufudumala ngezikhathi zokuhlangabeza inhlazane. Wafica unina uMaSikhakhane exhoza ummbila emahlezeni nokwabe kuzokwenziwa ngawo amahiyoyo. 
     "Shono nje ngidikizelelwa yiso kanjena kanti lingibikela wena ndodana yami Mashimane?" Kwasho uMaSikhakhane emoyizela izihlathi lezi zixosha izindlebe.

     "Tshela mina mntanami, yini ngempela lena enibusa ngayo kangaka kwelasezansi ebangela ukuba nidele ikhaya kanye nathi imbala sibe singonyoko?" 
     "Njengoba ungibona nje ngizokulanda mame, ukuze ube seduze kwami. Lo mbuw ongibuza wona impendulo yawo izoziqhashela ngokwayo."

Ngalolu suku ephuma ngayo ukuyozingela yilo futhi lolu suku abe esebuye ngalo ekhaya. Uthe esaluwela nje uThukela ngasezibukweni elingenhla wayibona inqina. Akusheshanga kwahlaluka ukuthi 'yinqina lena kuyena. Engqondweni kwasheshe kwafika ukuthi yimpi yimbe eyabe iphumele ukuyohlasela. Uthe angahlangana nabamaziyo ababeyingxenye yenqina walithola lonke iqiniso ngalo khukhulelangoqo owabe sewembethe ihlanze. Ibutho elikhulu abe ezogijima nalo kule nqina uMashimane kwabe kungamaPhela elabe Iizothatha iMpumalanga yeWanze. Akuqhubekanga sikhathi nesingakanani ithelwe yayekwa kwasuka lokho. Laqovumula ibhubesi ezansi nehlathi Ie kuzwakala nje ukuthi laselinukeIwa yigazi lezitha zalo elabe selilihogelile. Babodwa okwavele kwabamnyama amehlo kubo. Akekho owabuza komunye ukuthi kumele kwenziwenjani. Babodwa abafohloza babaleka kwaphuka izihlahla sebeqonde emfuleni ukuze bahlambe bawelele ngapheslfeya ngenhloso yokuphepha ezidladleni zengonyama. Babodwa abavele bacasha ngezikhotha nangezihlahla nangamafokozi wadlula ngezamahubo ebashiya ngemuva ufeleba lona. Ngale nkathi kwabe sekunguMashimane yedwa osehujwa yisilo lesi. Anele angabona naye ukuthi ayisengangaye, athi nombe emthini. Naye ufeleba lona akasaholobheli khona okwalapha Sekucishe kucacele noma ngubani ukuthi oyokwendulela ngaye useyokwendlalela abaningi. Nawo amathe lana okulinganiselwe ngokoma kwawo ukuvuthwa koselwa lwamakhosi, aya ngokwehla manje kulesi silinganiso ebesenziwe yinkosi. Sebeze bayikhiphela isicathulo samanzi amponjwana manje inkosi ukuze ithibe ilanga, nalo belu elizinika amandla phezu kwabo ngenxa yokushisa. Ithi nqebelezi bese isukuma ithathe umjikelezo ngalapho kwenziwe khona umqhudelwano woselwa lwamakhosi. Akubange kusapholiswa maseko. Yiso lesi isizwe senkosi sesibamba iNtshonaianga yezwe. Umfula uMthentweni sawuwelela enhla Sewusa imimango njalo saze sayohlaba ikhefu enWa nomfula iLovu. Akuvumanga ukuba selule isikhathi eside silapho ngoba izinhliziyo zase zilangazelele ukufinyelela lapho okhokho baso besiholela khona Sasuka futhi sathi khucu saluqhuba uhambo saze sayoqhamuka eBhekulwandle, kwezwakala isisho insingizi phezulu entabeni. Yasho kwangathi ihlola ilumbo. ¥mgoba lalibalele ngisho nasebukhweni bezinja ngalelo langa kungekho zimpawu zokuthi lingase lidume line. UMashimane wasidonsa isizwe sakhe esephikelele entabeni leyo yomsindo wokuqangalaza kwensingizi.

ISAHlUKO 21 

Uthinte Abangathintwa 

Kwase kuntambama kuNhlolanja seyiqala nokuphola inhlamvu yelanga. Uthe ukuba afike esigodlweni sakhe uMashimane wabe ekhinikelwa yindodana yakhe uMangcingci izinkulumo ezivuselana uhlevane ezihambisana nezinsongo okuthiwa ziphuma emlonyeni kaMakhutha. Usezwile nokuthi uMakhutha ndini lona ushokosha impi engase ihlasele noma yinini ukusukela ngosuku olulandelayo. 

     "Uhlekisa umootu ecashile phela wena ndodana. Khona sekuthiwa ngiphethwe yisithuthwane sengingatatazelela leli vukana elinguMakhutha pho? Ngabe sekuphele izinto engingazitatazelela yini?" Sekubuzisisa uMashimane. - 

     "Uthini ubaba bakithi? Ungambuki umuntu ebusweni bese uphelela lapho ngoba uyophoxeka lapho usuthola ukuthi akaseyona Ie nto owamgcina eyiyona. Awazi ukuthi wethembeni njengoba esezidele amathambo , wazimisela ngempi kadede nawe." Sekwenaba uMangcingci ngenkulumo. '. 

     "Ngisho ngabe ithemba lakhe ulibeke kubelumbi nezikhafulamlilo - zabo, kodwa akudikizi nqulu lapha kimi. Ngithi koqhuma gula Iinamasi.". 

Lezi zakhiwo zika-Adamu seziphakeme ngendlela esicacela yinoma ngubani manje ukuthi luhlobo looi lwezindlu oselwakhiwe. Izindlu zamasonto zehlukaniseka ngemibhoshongo nangophawu Iweziphambano kulezo eziyizikole. Kuthe sekuntambama selibantu bahle kwafika umbiko ngesigijimi ka-, Mashimane eNgoleleni uvela eMamba wokuthi unina kaMashimane intombi yakoSikhakhane seyendele kwelokhokho bayo. Kusukela ngaleyo mzuzu ukudla kwase kwehla ngomgogodla kuMashimane kwazise phela kwabe sekuxebuke isitho esikhulu emzimbeni wakhe uma eseshiywe ngunina owabe emkhonze ngenhliziyo yakhe yonke ngalolu hlobo. Isimo esinjengalesi samphoqa uMshimane ukuba ashiye phansi konke ayekwenza nayesazokwenza maqedane wathatha uhambo IwaseNyakatho esephikelele emanxiweni akubo amadaia. Yiso futhi lesi simo esaphoqa ukuba kugudluke usuku okwakuvunyelwene ngalo ukukhumelana umlotha phakathi kwezizwe ezimbili lube sosukwini olungaziwa. 

Ngale minyaka uMangcingci wabe esewthiwe eseyinsizwa emansansanana ngempela nesingabuthatha ubukhosi uma kuyangoba lisongwa igoda lempilo kayise. Kufanele sithi wabe eseyinsizwa esivuthiwe uMangcingci ngoba kwayena wabe esenendodana esiyibhojongwana ngale mihla ebizo layo kwabe kunguJ eqe. 

Kwaphela isikhathi esingangenyanga' yonke golokoqo ISlzwe senkosi, sisazilele ukwedlula emhlabeni kukanozaia wesizwe, kungaiinywa, isizwe . lesi sizithibile nasekwenzeni imisebenzi yezandla ethile enhlobonhlobo. Kwaginqwa ishumi lezinkomo khathi kwenziwe umsebenzi wehlambo nokuphelekezela inzalabantu yesizwe. 

Zase zelulekile izinsuku ngale minyaka nezindlu zokukhonza seziqalile ukuqhweba nokusondeza amakholwa ukuyokhonzela kuzo, kanti nezikole futhi zase ziqaiile ukumumatha izingane ngenhloso yokuzihlomisa ngezikhaii zemfundo nezempucuko, Kwase kuqala ukuntwela ezansi kuMashi- . mane ngoba sezibonakala izinguquko zenqubekela phambili esizweni ' ' sakhe nakuba umnyakazo wabe uhamba kancane kakhulu kwazise uMashimane wayengafuni ukwemukela ezinye izinguquko ezibukeka ziholela isizwe sakhe entuthukweni kanye nasenkanyisweni. Abefundisi kanye nabafundisi abaMhlophe basebetheleke ngokwezinkani kuleli ukuletha impucuko yaseNtshonalanga kwabendlu emnyama. Akukho okuthi kunesiqalo kodwa kungabi nasiphetho lapha phansi komthunzi welanga. Nohambo siyaluqala kodwa ekugcineni size sifinyelele esiphethweni salo. Ngokunjalo futhi ziyathokoza izidalwa zikaMvelinqangi ngenkathi zibona ilanga lisaphuma lintombi ngoba ziyazi ukuthi ukuqala kwalo uhambo kuletha ukukhanya nokufudumala kuyo yonke imvelo. Kuwo wonke lowo mjikelezo wohambo zisuke zazi ukuthi ukushona kWalo selinsizwa kuchaza isiphetho salo ngalolo lusuku esisuke sesinciphise kumbe saqeda amathuba entokozo, ngenxa yokuthi kusuke sekulindeleke ubumnyama mhlawumbe njalo futhi namakhaza. Zikhona futhi izimo lapho into sike siyibone ukuqala kwayo kodwa isiphetho sayo singabi yile nto ebilindelekile. Kuba Kuhle nokho uma sizothi siqala siyibona into yenzeka, kodwa siphinde siyihambele phambili futhi ngokwesiphetho yize ingakafmyeleli kuso nakhona lokho sikwenze ngendlela enembayo ehlaba emhlolweni. 

     "Mangcingci. Igxathu elilandelayo mfana wami ngelokugcoba wena esihlalweni sobukhosi kuse kuhle nje. Angizimisele neze ukuba ngize ngificwe wubumnyama singakafezeki lesi sifiso sami. Ngakho-ke ngibona sekufanele manje ukuba ngiqoqe isizwe maqedane ngisazise ngosuku engilumisayo ukukunika indawo yakho." 
     "Angiyiboni ngeso oyibuka ngalo Ie nto mina baba. Mina ngibona useyingqabavu yensizwa nje wena ngokunjalo futhi usafanele wukugijima elinye ibanga elide elicishe libe ngangaleli osuligijimile nesizwe. Ngivumele noma ungiphikise baba uma ngithi iziphiwo zabantu kazifani. Ngala mazwi ngilanda ukuthi isizwe sesejwayele isandla sakho njengesiyiso nesifanele ukuphatha abantu. Cabanga-ke nje ukuthi mkhulu kangakanani umehluko phakathi kwaleli klume eliyimina uma ngabe' selibekelwe umgomo wokugijima ibanga lezinsizwa esezimnkantshubomvu njengawe nje Zikode omkhulu." Sekuphendula uMangcingci.

130. 
131. 

UMashimane wawuqopha umlando etsheni wayibeka induku ebandla kubantu bozalo lwakubo. Waba yisibani esingasoze sacisha ezizukulwaneni zakwaMaphumulo kuwo womane amagumbi omhlaba. Igama lakhe alisoze lalibaleka emlandweni phakathi kwamaqhawe aziwayo kwelengabadi. Ukukhothama kwakhe kwabe sekuwukuqhekezeka komfantu ongasophinde wanamekeka ngoba isizwe samazikode sabe sesilahlekelwe kakhulu. 

Kusuke sekonakele ngempela ungaze uzwe umuntu wakwaMaphumulo esethi: "Ngimfunge uMashimane eseNgoleleni." Ngisho ngabe ngowesilisa, ngisho ngabe owesifazane osefunge kanjalo, kumele wehlele ngezansi " uxolise uma ngabe nixabene, umyeke adlondlobale yena. Kungagcini lapho futhi. Uphinde uqhele eduze kwakhe, ngoba uma ulokhu uqophisana naye ngamazwi usungaze ulutheze olunenkume. 

Umuntu wakwaMaphumulo wadonswa ngezindlebe ukuba angalokothi neze aliphathe ngeze igama IikaMashimane. Yingakho-ke nje uma umuntu walesi sibongo esefunge uMashimane usuke ezokuyabula akushaye ngempela akushiye nesibazi esiyinkambabeyibuza kumbe umvimbo, noma akubulale ufe nya uma umdazisa inkani. Ngokunjalo futhi sisuke sizoyifeza inhloso isiqalekiso sakhe uma ngabe umuntu wakwaMaphumulo esencinde umunwe wenza nophawu lwesiphambano maqedane wagagula igama likaMashimane. Kudela owaziyo ukuthi usayoqhamuka yini omunye ezizukulwaneni zakwaMaphumulo oyovelela abe negalelo eliyokwenza igama lakhe lifungwe njengoMashimane.
